seconds\n- Sends pipeline execution metrics\n- Receives configuration updates\n\n**Ninja Integration**:\n- Monitored for errors and performance issues\n- Auto-healing for failed pipelines\n- Performance optimization recommendations\n- Dependency management\n\n**Standalone Mode**:\n- Can operate without Hub connection\n- Local configuration management\n- File-based logging\n- Manual pipeline management\n\n---\n\n## üöÄ Core Features\n\n### 1. Data Ingestion (100+ Connectors)\n\n#### Databases\n- **Relational**: PostgreSQL, MySQL, SQL Server, Oracle, MariaDB\n- **NoSQL**: MongoDB, Cassandra, Redis, DynamoDB, Couchbase\n- **Data Warehouses**: Snowflake, Redshift, BigQuery, Synapse\n- **Time Series**: InfluxDB, TimescaleDB, Prometheus\n\n#### Cloud Services\n- **AWS**: S3, RDS, DynamoDB, Kinesis, SQS, SNS\n- **Azure**: Blob Storage, SQL Database, Cosmos DB, Event Hubs\n- **GCP**: Cloud Storage, BigQuery, Pub/Sub, Firestore\n\n#### APIs & Protocols\n- REST APIs with authentication (OAuth, API Key, Basic)\n- GraphQL endpoints\n- SOAP services\n- gRPC services\n- WebSocket streams\n\n#### File Systems\n- Local file systems\n- Network file systems (NFS, SMB)\n- SFTP/FTP servers\n- Cloud storage (S3, Azure Blob, GCS)\n\n#### Streaming Platforms\n- Apache Kafka\n- Apache Pulsar\n- RabbitMQ\n- AWS Kinesis\n- Azure Event Hubs\n- Google Pub/Sub\n\n#### SaaS Applications\n- Salesforce\n- HubSpot\n- Zendesk\n- Jira\n- Slack\n- Microsoft 365\n- Google Workspace\n\n### 2. Data Transformation\n\n#### Built-in Transformations\n- **Data Cleansing**: Remove duplicates, handle nulls, trim whitespace\n- **Data Validation**: Type checking, range validation, format validation\n- **Data Enrichment**: Lookup tables, API enrichment, geocoding\n- **Data Aggregation**: Group by, sum, average, count, min, max\n- **Data Filtering**: Conditional filtering, pattern matching\n- **Data Mapping**: Column mapping, type conversion, value mapping\n- **Data Splitting**: Split columns, parse JSON/XML, extract patterns\n- **Data Joining**: Inner, outer, left, right joins\n\n#### Custom Transformations\n- Python-based custom transformations\n- SQL-based transformations\n- JavaScript transformations\n- Regex-based transformations\n\n### 3. Data Loading\n\n#### Batch Loading\n- Bulk insert operations\n- Upsert (insert or update)\n- Incremental loading\n- Full refresh loading\n- Partitioned loading\n\n#### Streaming Loading\n- Real-time data streaming\n- Micro-batch processing\n- Change data capture (CDC)\n- Event-driven loading\n\n#### Loading Strategies\n- **Append**: Add new records\n- **Overwrite**: Replace existing data\n- **Merge**: Update existing, insert new\n- **SCD Type 2**: Maintain history with versioning\n\n### 4. Data Quality & Validation\n\n#### Quality Checks\n- **Completeness**: Check for missing values\n- **Accuracy**: Validate against reference data\n- **Consistency**: Cross-field validation\n- **Timeliness**: Check data freshness\n- **Uniqueness**: Detect duplicates\n- **Validity**: Format and type validation\n\n#### Quality Actions\n- **Alert**: Notify on quality issues\n- **Quarantine**: Move bad records to quarantine\n- **Reject**: Stop pipeline on critical issues\n- **Auto-Fix**: Attempt automatic correction\n- **Log**: Record quality issues for review\n\n### 5. Schema Evolution\n\n#### Automatic Handling\n- Detect schema changes in source\n- Add new columns automatically\n- Handle column type changes\n- Manage column renames\n- Track schema versions\n\n#### Schema Validation\n- Validate against expected schema\n- Alert on breaking changes\n- Rollback on incompatible changes\n- Version control for schemas\n\n### 6. Data Lineage\n\n#### Lineage Tracking\n- Source to destination tracking\n- Transformation history\n- Data flow visualization\n- Impact analysis\n- Dependency mapping\n\n#### Lineage Queries\n- Find data origin\n- Track data usage\n- Identify downstream impacts\n- Audit data transformations\n\n### 7. Self-Healing Pipelines\n\n#### Error Detection\n- Connection failures\n- Data quality issues\n- Transformation errors\n- Loading failures\n- Performance degradation\n\n#### Auto-Recovery\n- Automatic retry with exponential backoff\n- Circuit breaker pattern\n- Fallback to alternative sources\n- Data replay from checkpoints\n- Notification to Ninja for complex issues\n\n---\n\n## üîå API Reference\n\n### Pipeline Management\n\n#### Create Pipeline\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/pipelines\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "name": "customer_data_sync",\n  "description": "Sync customer data from CRM to warehouse",\n  "source": {\n    "type": "salesforce",\n    "config": {\n      "object": "Account",\n      "fields": ["Id", "Name", "Email", "CreatedDate"]\n    }\n  },\n  "transformations": [\n    {\n      "type": "filter",\n      "condition": "CreatedDate > \'2024-01-01\'"\n    },\n    {\n      "type": "map",\n      "mappings": {\n        "Id": "customer_id",\n        "Name": "customer_name",\n        "Email": "email"\n      }\n    }\n  ],\n  "destination": {\n    "type": "postgresql",\n    "config": {\n      "table": "customers",\n      "mode": "upsert",\n      "key": "customer_id"\n    }\n  },\n  "schedule": "0 */6 * * *",\n  "quality_checks": [\n    {\n      "type": "not_null",\n      "columns": ["customer_id", "email"]\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n#### Execute Pipeline\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/pipelines/{pipeline_id}/execute\n```\n\n#### Get Pipeline Status\n```http\nGET /api/v1/pipelines/{pipeline_id}/status\n```\n\n#### Get Pipeline Metrics\n```http\nGET /api/v1/pipelines/{pipeline_id}/metrics\n```\n\n### Connector Management\n\n#### List Available Connectors\n```http\nGET /api/v1/connectors\n```\n\n#### Test Connection\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/connectors/test\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "type": "postgresql",\n  "config": {\n    "host": "localhost",\n    "port": 5432,\n    "database": "mydb",\n    "username": "user",\n    "password": "pass"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Data Quality\n\n#### Run Quality Checks\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/quality/check\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "pipeline_id": "pipeline_123",\n  "checks": [\n    {\n      "type": "completeness",\n      "threshold": 0.95\n    },\n    {\n      "type": "uniqueness",\n      "columns": ["customer_id"]\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n#### Get Quality Report\n```http\nGET /api/v1/quality/report/{pipeline_id}\n```\n\n### Lineage\n\n#### Get Data Lineage\n```http\nGET /api/v1/lineage/{dataset_id}\n```\n\n#### Get Impact Analysis\n```http\nGET /api/v1/lineage/{dataset_id}/impact\n```\n\n---\n\n## üîß Configuration\n\n### Environment Variables\n\n```bash\n# Database Configuration\nDATAFLOW_DB_HOST=localhost\nDATAFLOW_DB_PORT=5432\nDATAFLOW_DB_NAME=dataflow\nDATAFLOW_DB_USER=dataflow_user\nDATAFLOW_DB_PASSWORD=secure_password\n\n# Redis Configuration (for caching Integration\nDATAFLOW_NINJA_URL=http://ninja:8000\nDATAFLOW_NINJA_API_KEY=ninja_api_key\nDATAFLOW_NINJA_ENABLED=true\n\n# Standalone Mode\nDATAFLOW_STANDALONE_MODE=false\n\n# Performance Settings\nDATAFLOW_MAX_WORKERS=10\nDATAFLOW_BATCH_SIZE=1000\nDATAFLOW_RETRY_ATTEMPTS=3\nDATAFLOW_RETRY_DELAY=5\n\n# Logging\nDATAFLOW_LOG_LEVEL=INFO\nDATAFLOW_LOG_FORMAT=json\n```\n\n### Configuration File (config.yaml)\n\n```yaml\ndataflow:\n  # General Settings\n  name: "iTechSmart DataFlow"\n  version: "1.0.0"\n  \n  # Database\n  database:\n    host: "${DATAFLOW_DB_HOST}"\n    port: ${DATAFLOW_DB_PORT}\n    name: "${DATAFLOW_DB_NAME}"\n    user: "${DATAFLOW_DB_USER}"\n    password: "${DATAFLOW_DB_PASSWORD}"\n    pool_size: 20\n    max_overflow: 10\n  \n  # Redis\n  redis:\n    host: "${DATAFLOW_REDIS_HOST}"\n    port: ${DATAFLOW_REDIS_PORT}\n    password: "${DATAFLOW_REDIS_PASSWORD}"\n    db: 0\n  \n  # Kafka\n  kafka:\n    brokers: "${DATAFLOW_KAFKA_BROKERS}"\n    topic_prefix: "${DATAFLOW_KAFKA_TOPIC_PREFIX}"\n    consumer_group: "dataflow-consumers"\n  \n  # Enterprise Hub\n  hub:\n    enabled: ${DATAFLOW_HUB_ENABLED}\n    url: "${DATAFLOW_HUB_URL}"\n    api_key: "${DATAFLOW_HUB_API_KEY}"\n    health_check_interval: 30\n    metrics_interval: 60\n  \n  # Ninja Integration\n  ninja:\n    enabled: ${DATAFLOW_NINJA_ENABLED}\n    url: "${DATAFLOW_NINJA_URL}"\n    api_key: "${DATAFLOW_NINJA_API_KEY}"\n    error_threshold: 5\n    performance_threshold: 0.8\n  \n  # Performance\n  performance:\n    max_workers: ${DATAFLOW_MAX_WORKERS}\n    batch_size: ${DATAFLOW_BATCH_SIZE}\n    retry_attempts: ${DATAFLOW_RETRY_ATTEMPTS}\n    retry_delay: ${DATAFLOW_RETRY_DELAY}\n    timeout: 300\n  \n  # Quality\n  quality:\n    enabled: true\n    default_threshold: 0.95\n    quarantine_enabled: true\n    auto_fix_enabled: true\n```\n\n---\n\n## üöÄ Quick Start\n\n### Installation\n\n#### Using migrations\nalembic upgrade head\n\n# Start the service\npython -m app.main\n```\n\n### Creating Your First Pipeline\n\n```python\nimport requests\n\n# Create a simple pipeline\npipeline = {\n    "name": "csv_to_postgres",\n    "source": {\n        "type": "csv",\n        "config": {\n            "path": "/data/customers.csv",\n            "delimiter": ",",\n            "header": True\n        }\n    },\n    "transformations": [\n        {\n            "type": "filter",\n            "condition": "age > 18"\n        }\n    ],\n    "destination": {\n        "type": "postgresql",\n        "config": {\n            "table": "customers",\n            "mode": "append"\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n# Create the pipeline\nresponse = requests.post(\n    "http://localhost:8080/api/v1/pipelines",\n    json=pipeline,\n    headers={"Authorization": "Bearer YOUR_API_KEY"}\n)\n\npipeline_id = response.json()["id"]\n\n# Execute the pipeline\nrequests.post(\n    f"http://localhost:8080/api/v1/pipelines/{pipeline_id}/execute",\n    headers={"Authorization": "Bearer YOUR_API_KEY"}\n)\n```\n\n---\n\n## üîó Integration Points\n\n### Enterprise Hub Enterprise Hub on startup\n- Reports analytics metrics and usage\n- Receives configuration updates\n- Shares insights across products\n\n**Ninja Integration**:\n- Monitored for performance issues\n- Auto-optimization of queries\n- Cache management\n- Resource optimization\n\n**DataFlow Integration**:\n- Receives data from DataFlow pipelines\n- Real-time data streaming\n- Historical data access\n- Data quality metrics\n\n**Standalone Mode**:\n- Can operate without Hub connection\n- Local data sources\n- File-based configuration\n- Offline analytics\n\n---\n\n## üöÄ Core Features\n\n### 1. Real-Time Dashboards\n\n#### Dashboard Types\n- **Executive Dashboards**: High-level KPIs and trends\n- **Operational Dashboards**: Real-time operational metrics\n- **Analytical Dashboards**: Deep-dive analysis and exploration\n- **Custom Dashboards**: User-created dashboards\n\n#### Widget Types\n- **Line Charts**: Time-series data visualization\n- **Bar Charts**: Categorical comparisons\n- **Pie Charts**: Proportional data\n- **Area Charts**: Cumulative trends\n- **Scatter Plots**: Correlation analysis\n- **Heatmaps**: Multi-dimensional data\n- **Tables**: Detailed data views\n- **Metric Cards**: Single KPI display\n- **Gauges**: Progress and targets\n- **Funnels**: Conversion analysis\n- **Treemaps**: Hierarchical data\n- **Sankey Diagrams**: Flow visualization\n\n#### Dashboard Features\n- **Drag-and-Drop Builder**: Visual dashboard creation\n- **Real-Time Updates**: WebSocket-based live updates\n- **Responsive Design**: Mobile and desktop optimized\n- **Drill-Down**: Interactive data exploration\n- **Filters**: Dynamic filtering and slicing\n- **Time Range Selection**: Flexible time periods\n- **Export**: PDF, PNG, Excel, CSV exports\n- **Sharing**: Share dashboards via link or embed\n\n### 2. Predictive Analytics\n\n#### Forecasting Models\n- **Time Series Forecasting**: ARIMA, Prophet, LSTM\n- **Regression Analysis**: Linear, polynomial, logistic\n- **Classification**: Decision trees, random forests, neural networks\n- **Clustering**: K-means, hierarchical, DBSCAN\n- **Anomaly Detection**: Isolation forest, autoencoders\n\n#### Predictive Features\n- **Trend Analysis**: Identify trends and patterns\n- **Seasonality Detection**: Detect seasonal patterns\n- **Outlier Detection**: Identify anomalies\n- **What-If Analysis**: Scenario modeling\n- **Confidence Intervals**: Prediction uncertainty\n- **Model Comparison**: Compare multiple models\n\n### 3. Natural Language Queries\n\n#### Query Capabilities\n- **Ask Questions**: "What were sales last quarter?"\n- **Compare Metrics**: "Compare revenue this year vs last year"\n- **Find Insights**: "Show me top performing products"\n- **Trend Analysis**: "What\'s the trend in customer churn?"\n- **Drill Down**: "Break down by region and product"\n\n#### NL Features\n- **Context Awareness**: Understands business context\n- **Multi-Turn Conversations**: Follow-up questions\n- **Suggestions**: Query suggestions based on data\n- **Clarification**: Asks for clarification when needed\n- **Learning**: Improves from user interactions\n\n### 4. AI-Powered Insights\n\n#### Automated Insights\n- **Anomaly Alerts**: Automatic detection of unusual patterns\n- **Trend Notifications**: Alert on significant trends\n- **Correlation Discovery**: Find hidden relationships\n- **Segment Analysis**: Identify key segments\n- **Performance Alerts**: Notify on KPI changes\n\n#### Insight Types\n- **Descriptive**: What happened?\n- **Diagnostic**: Why did it happen?\n- **Predictive**: What will happen?\n- **Prescriptive**: What should we do?\n\n### 5. Custom Report Builder\n\n#### Report Types\n- **Scheduled Reports**: Automated report generation\n- **Ad-Hoc Reports**: On-demand reporting\n- **Interactive Reports**: Drill-down and filtering\n- **Pixel-Perfect Reports**: Formatted for printing\n\n#### Report Features\n- **Visual Builder**: Drag-and-drop report design\n- **Templates**: Pre-built report templates\n- **Formatting**: Rich text formatting\n- **Calculations**: Custom calculations and formulas\n- **Grouping**: Group and aggregate data\n- **Sorting**: Multi-level sorting\n- **Conditional Formatting**: Highlight important data\n\n#### Export Formats\n- PDF with custom branding\n- Excel with multiple sheets\n- CSV for data analysis\n- HTML for web viewing\n- PowerPoint for presentations\n\n### 6. application/json\n\n{\n  "name": "Sales Performance",\n  "description": "Real-time sales metrics",\n  "layout": {\n    "widgets": [\n      {\n        "type": "metric_card",\n        "title": "Total Revenue",\n        "query": "SELECT SUM(amount) FROM sales WHERE date >= NOW() - INTERVAL \'30 days\'",\n        "position": {"x": 0, "y": 0, "w": 3, "h": 2}\n      },\n      {\n        "type": "line_chart",\n        "title": "Revenue Trend",\n        "query": "SELECT DATE(date) as date, SUM(amount) as revenue FROM sales WHERE date >= NOW() - INTERVAL \'90 days\' GROUP BY DATE(date)",\n        "position": {"x": 3, "y": 0, "w": 9, "h": 4}\n      }\n    ]\n  },\n  "refresh_interval": 30,\n  "filters": [\n    {\n      "field": "region",\n      "type": "select",\n      "options": ["North", "South", "East", "West"]\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n#### Get Dashboard\n```http\nGET /api/v1/dashboards/{dashboard_id}\n```\n\n#### Update Dashboard\n```http\nPUT /api/v1/dashboards/{dashboard_id}\n```\n\n### Natural Language Queries\n\n#### Ask Question\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/nl/query\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "question": "What were total sales last quarter?",\n  "context": {\n    "user_id": "user_123",\n    "organization_id": "org_456"\n  }\n}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "answer": "Total sales last quarter were $1,234,567",\n  "sql": "SELECT SUM(amount) FROM sales WHERE date >= \'2024-10-01\' AND date < \'2025-01-01\'",\n  "visualization": {\n    "type": "metric_card",\n    "value": 1234567,\n    "format": "currency"\n  },\n  "confidence": 0.95\n}\n```\n\n### Predictive Analytics\n\n#### Create Forecast\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/analytics/forecast\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "metric": "revenue",\n  "data_source": "sales",\n  "model": "prophet",\n  "forecast_periods": 30,\n  "confidence_interval": 0.95\n}\n```\n\n#### Get Insights\n```http\nGET /api/v1/analytics/insights?dashboard_id={dashboard_id}\n```\n\n### Report Generation\n\n#### Generate Report\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/reports/generate\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "template_id": "monthly_sales",\n  "format": "pdf",\n  "parameters": {\n    "start_date": "2024-01-01",\n    "end_date": "2024-01-31",\n    "region": "North"\n  },\n  "delivery": {\n    "method": "email",\n    "recipients": ["manager@company.com"]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Alerts\n\n#### Create Alert\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/alerts\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "name": "High Revenue Alert",\n  "condition": {\n    "metric": "daily_revenue",\n    "operator": "greater_than",\n    "threshold": 100000\n  },\n  "channels": ["email", "slack"],\n  "recipients": ["sales@company.com"],\n  "frequency": "immediate"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## üîß Configuration\n\n### Dashboard\n\n```python\nimport requests\n\n# Create a dashboard\ndashboard = {\n    "name": "Sales Dashboard",\n    "description": "Real-time sales metrics",\n    "layout": {\n        "widgets": [\n            {\n                "type": "metric_card",\n                "title": "Total Revenue",\n                "query": "SELECT SUM(amount) FROM sales",\n                "position": {"x": 0, "y": 0, "w": 3, "h": 2}\n            },\n            {\n                "type": "line_chart",\n                "title": "Daily Revenue",\n                "query": "SELECT date, SUM(amount) FROM sales GROUP BY json=dashboard,\n    headers={"Authorization": "Bearer YOUR_API_KEY"}\n)\n\ndashboard_id = response.json()["id"]\nprint(f"Dashboard created: {dashboard_id}")\n```\n\n### Using Natural Language Receives configuration updates\n- Manages API access across products\n\n**Ninja Integration**:\n- Monitored for performance issues\n- Auto-scaling based on load\n- Error detection and recovery\n- Performance optimization\n\n**PassPort Integration**:\n- API authentication and authorization\n- OAuth 2.0 and JWT support\n- API key management\n- Service-to-service authentication\n\n**Standalone Mode**:\n- Can operate without Hub connection\n- Local API management\n- File-based configuration\n- Offline API gateway\n\n---\n\n## üöÄ Core Features\n\n### 1. API Gateway\n\n#### Gateway Capabilities\n- **Request Routing**: Intelligent routing to backend services\n- **Load Balancing**: Distribute traffic across instances\n- **Protocol Translation**: REST, GraphQL, gRPC, SOAP\n- **Request/Response Transformation**: Modify headers, body, parameters\n- **Caching**: Response caching for improved performance\n- **Compression**: Automatic response compression\n- **CORS Handling**: Cross-origin resource sharing\n- **SSL/TLS Termination**: Secure connections\n\n#### Routing Features\n- **Path-based Routing**: Route by URL path\n- **Header-based Routing**: Route by HTTP headers\n- **Query Parameter Routing**: Route by query parameters\n- **Host-based Routing**: Route by hostname\n- **Method-based Routing**: Route by HTTP method\n- **Weighted Routing**: A/B testing and canary deployments\n- **Failover Routing**: Automatic failover to backup services\n\n### 2. Rate Limiting & Throttling\n\n#### Rate Limiting Strategies\n- **Fixed Window**: Requests per time window\n- **Sliding Window**: Rolling time window\n- **Token Bucket**: Burst handling\n- **Leaky Bucket**: Smooth rate limiting\n- **Concurrent Requests**: Limit simultaneous requests\n\n#### Throttling Levels\n- **Global**: Apply to all APIs\n- **Per API**: Specific limits per API\n- **Per User**: User-specific limits\n- **Per IP**: IP-based limits\n- **Per API Key**: Key-specific limits\n\n#### Rate Limit Features\n- **Custom Headers**: X-RateLimit headers\n- **Quota Management**: Monthly/daily quotas\n- **Burst Allowance**: Handle traffic spikes\n- **Rate Limit Bypass**: Whitelist trusted clients\n- **Dynamic Limits**: Adjust based on load\n\n### 3. API Versioning\n\n#### Versioning Strategies\n- **URL Path Versioning**: /v1/users, /v2/users\n- **Header Versioning**: Accept: application/vnd.api.v1+json\n- **Query Parameter Versioning**: /users?version=1\n- **Content Negotiation**: Accept header versioning\n\n#### Version Management\n- **Multiple Active Versions**: Run multiple versions simultaneously\n- **Version Deprecation**: Gradual version sunset\n- **Version Migration**: Automated migration tools\n- **Backward Compatibility**: Maintain compatibility\n- **Version Analytics**: Track version usage\n\n### 4. Developer Portal\n\n#### Portal Features\n- **API Documentation**: Interactive API docs (OpenAPI/Swagger)\n- **API Explorer**: Test APIs directly in browser\n- **Code Samples**: Auto-generated code in multiple languages\n- **API Key Management**: Self-service API key creation\n- **Usage Dashboard**: View API usage and quotas\n- **Support Tickets**: Integrated support system\n- **API Changelog**: Track API changes\n\n#### Documentation Features\n- **Auto-generated Docs**: From OpenAPI specs\n- **Interactive Examples**: Try API calls\n- **Authentication Guide**: Setup instructions\n- **Error Reference**: Complete error documentation\n- **Best Practices**: API usage guidelines\n- **Tutorials**: Step-by-step guides\n\n### 5. GraphQL Support\n\n#### GraphQL Features\n- **Schema Management**: Define and manage GraphQL schemas\n- **Query Optimization**: Automatic query optimization\n- **Batching**: Batch multiple queries\n- **Caching**: Query result caching\n- **Subscriptions**: Real-time data with WebSocket\n- **Federation**: Combine multiple GraphQL services\n\n#### GraphQL Tools\n- **GraphQL Playground**: Interactive query editor\n- **Schema Stitching**: Combine multiple schemas\n- **Query Complexity Analysis**: Prevent expensive queries\n- **Persisted Queries**: Pre-approved queries\n- **Query Whitelisting**: Security through approved queries\n\n### 6. Webhook Management\n\n#### Webhook Features\n- **Event Subscriptions**: Subscribe to API events\n- **Webhook Delivery**: Reliable delivery with retries\n- **Webhook Security**: HMAC signature verification\n- **Webhook Testing**: Test webhooks before deployment\n- **Webhook Logs**: Complete delivery logs\n- **Webhook Replay**: Replay failed webhooks\n\n#### Event Types\n- **API Events**: API calls, errors, rate limits\n- **Resource Events**: Create, update, delete\n- **System Events**: Service status, maintenance\n- **Custom Events**: User-defined events\n\n### 7. API Analytics\n\n#### Analytics Metrics\n- **Request Volume**: Total requests over time\n- **Response Times**: Latency percentiles (P50, P95, P99)\n- **Error Rates**: 4xx and 5xx errors\n- **Success Rates**: Successful requests\n- **Bandwidth Usage**: Data transfer metrics\n- **Top Endpoints**: Most used APIs\n- **Top Consumers**: Most active users\n- **Geographic Distribution**: Requests by location\n\n#### Analytics Features\n- **Real-Time Dashboards**: Live metrics\n- **Historical Analysis**: Trend analysis\n- **Custom Reports**: Build custom reports\n- **Alerts**: Threshold-based alerts\n- **Export**: CSV, JSON, PDF exports\n- **API Health Score**: Overall API health\n\n### 8. API Marketplace\n\n#### Marketplace Features\n- **API Catalog**: Browse available APIs\n- **API Discovery**: Search and filter APIs\n- **API Ratings**: User ratings and reviews\n- **API Pricing**: Monetization support\n- **API Subscriptions**: Subscribe to APIs\n- **API Trials**: Free trial periods\n\n---\n\n## üîå API Reference\n\n### API Management\n\n#### Create API\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/apis\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "name": "User Management API",\n  "version": "v1",\n  "base_path": "/api/v1/users",\n  "backend_url": "http://user-service:8080",\n  "authentication": {\n    "type": "jwt",\n    "required": true\n  },\n  "rate_limit": {\n    "requests_per_minute": 100,\n    "burst": 20\n  },\n  "endpoints": [\n    {\n      "path": "/",\n      "method": "GET",\n      "description": "List all users",\n      "public": false\n    },\n    {\n      "path": "/{id}",\n      "method": "GET",\n      "description": "Get user by ID",\n      "public": false\n    },\n    {\n      "path": "/",\n      "method": "POST",\n      "description": "Create new user",\n      "public": false\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n#### Update API\n```http\nPUT /api/v1/apis/{api_id}\n```\n\n#### Delete API\n```http\nDELETE /api/v1/apis/{api_id}\n```\n\n#### Get API Metrics\n```http\nGET /api/v1/apis/{api_id}/metrics?start_date=2024-01-01&end_date=2024-01-31\n```\n\n### Rate Limiting\n\n#### Set Rate Limit\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/rate-limits\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "api_id": "api_123",\n  "strategy": "sliding_window",\n  "limit": 1000,\n  "window": "1h",\n  "scope": "per_user"\n}\n```\n\n#### Get Rate Limit Status\n```http\nGET /api/v1/rate-limits/status?api_key={api_key}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "limit": 1000,\n  "remaining": 847,\n  "reset": "2024-01-15T14:00:00Z",\n  "window": "1h"\n}\n```\n\n### API Keys\n\n#### Create API Key\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/api-keys\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "name": "Production Key",\n  "scopes": ["users:read", "users:write"],\n  "rate_limit": {\n    "requests_per_minute": 100\n  },\n  "expires_at": "2025-12-31T23:59:59Z"\n}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "id": "key_123",\n  "key": "sk_live_abc123xyz789",\n  "name": "Production Key",\n  "created_at": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z"\n}\n```\n\n#### Revoke API Key\n```http\nDELETE /api/v1/api-keys/{key_id}\n```\n\n### Webhooks\n\n#### Create Webhook\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/webhooks\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "url": "https://example.com/webhook",\n  "events": ["api.request", "api.error"],\n  "secret": "webhook_secret_123",\n  "active": true\n}\n```\n\n#### Test Webhook\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/webhooks/{webhook_id}/test\n```\n\n### GraphQL\n\n#### Execute GraphQL Query\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/graphql\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "query": "query { users { id name email }  ‚îÇ                  ‚îÇ iTechSmart Ninja‚îÇ\n‚îÇ  (Monitoring)   ‚îÇ                  ‚îÇ  (Self-Healing) ‚îÇ\n‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò metrics\n- Centralized secret management\n- Cross-product secret sharing\n\n**Ninja Integration**:\n- Monitored for security issues\n- Auto-rotation of compromised secrets\n- Performance optimization\n- Backup and recovery\n\n**PassPort Integration**:\n- Authentication for vault access\n- User and service identity\n- Role-based access control\n- Multi-factor authentication\n\n**Standalone Mode**:\n- Can operate without Hub connection\n- Local secret storage\n- File-based configuration\n- Offline secret management\n\n---\n\n## üöÄ Core Features\n\n### 1. Encrypted Secrets Storage\n\n#### Storage Features\n- **AES-256 Encryption**: Military-grade encryption\n- **Encryption at Rest**: All data encrypted on disk\n- **Encryption in Transit**: TLS 1.3 for all communications\n- **Key Versioning**: Multiple versions of secrets\n- **Soft Delete**: Recover deleted secrets\n- **Secret Metadata**: Tags, descriptions, expiration\n\n#### Secret Types\n- **Key-Value Secrets**: Simple key-value pairs\n- **JSON Secrets**: Structured JSON data\n- **Binary Secrets**: Files and certificates\n- **Environment Variables**: Application configuration\n- **Database Credentials**: Connection strings\n- **API Keys**: Third-party API keys\n- **SSH Keys**: SSH private keys\n- **Certificates**: SSL/TLS certificates\n\n#### Storage Backends\n- **PostgreSQL**: Default storage backend\n- **AWS S3**: Cloud storage with encryption\n- **Azure Key Vault**: Native Azure integration\n- **GCP Secret Manager**: Native GCP integration\n- **HashiCorp Vault**: Compatible with Vault protocol\n- **File System**: Local encrypted storage\n\n### 2. Dynamic Secrets\n\n#### Dynamic Secret Types\n- **Database Credentials**: Temporary database users\n- **Cloud Credentials**: Temporary cloud access keys\n- **API Tokens**: Short-lived API tokens\n- **SSH Certificates**: Temporary SSH access\n- **PKI Certificates**: On-demand certificates\n\n#### Dynamic Secret Features\n- **On-Demand Generation**: Create secrets when needed\n- **Automatic Expiration**: Secrets expire automatically\n- **Lease Management**: Extend or revoke leases\n- **Revocation**: Immediately revoke access\n- **Renewal**: Extend secret lifetime\n\n#### Supported Systems\n- **Databases**: PostgreSQL, MySQL, MongoDB, Redis\n- **Cloud Providers**: AWS, Azure, GCP\n- **SSH**: OpenSSH certificate authority\n- **PKI**: X.509 certificate authority\n- **Active Directory**: AD user management\n\n### 3. Automatic Rotation\n\n#### Rotation Strategies\n- **Time-Based**: Rotate on schedule\n- **Event-Based**: Rotate on specific events\n- **Manual**: On-demand rotation\n- **Automatic**: Detect and rotate compromised secrets\n\n#### Rotation Features\n- **Zero-Downtime**: Rotate without service interruption\n- **Rollback**: Revert to previous version\n- **Notification**: Alert on rotation\n- **Verification**: Test new secrets before activation\n- **Coordination**: Coordinate rotation across services\n\n#### Rotatable Secrets\n- Database passwords\n- API keys\n- Encryption keys\n- Certificates\n- Cloud credentials\n- Service account keys\n\n### 4. Access Policies\n\n#### Policy Types\n- **Path-Based**: Control access by secret path\n- **Role-Based**: Assign roles to users/services\n- **Attribute-Based**: Dynamic policies based on attributes\n- **Time-Based**: Temporary access grants\n- **IP-Based**: Restrict by IP address\n\n#### Policy Features\n- **Fine-Grained Control**: Precise permissions\n- **Policy Templates**: Pre-built policy templates\n- **Policy Inheritance**: Hierarchical policies\n- **Policy Validation**: Test policies before applying\n- **Policy Versioning**: Track policy changes\n\n#### Permission Types\n- **Read**: View secret values\n- **Write**: Create/update secrets\n- **Delete**: Remove secrets\n- **List**: List available secrets\n- **Rotate**: Trigger rotation\n- **Admin**: Full control\n\n### 5. Audit Logging\n\n#### Audit Events\n- **Secret Access**: Who accessed what and when\n- **Secret Changes**: Create, update, delete operations\n- **Policy Changes**: Policy modifications\n- **Authentication**: Login attempts and failures\n- **Authorization**: Permission checks\n- **Rotation Events**: Secret rotation activities\n\n#### Audit Features\n- **Immutable Logs**: Cannot be modified or deleted\n- **Tamper Detection**: Cryptographic verification\n- **Log Retention**: Configurable retention periods\n- **Log Export**: Export to SIEM systems\n- **Real-Time Alerts**: Immediate notification\n- **Compliance Reports**: Pre-built compliance reports\n\n#### Compliance Standards\n- **SOC 2**: SOC 2 Type II compliance\n- **HIPAA**: Healthcare compliance\n- **PCI DSS**: Payment card compliance\n- **GDPR**: Data privacy compliance\n- **ISO 27001**: Information security\n\n### 6. Multi-Cloud Support\n\n#### Cloud Integrations\n- **AWS Secrets Manager**: Native AWS integration\n- **AWS KMS**: Key management service\n- **Azure Key Vault**: Native Azure integration\n- **Azure Managed Identity**: Azure authentication\n- **GCP Secret Manager**: Native GCP integration\n- **GCP KMS**: Key management service\n\n#### Cloud Features\n- **Cloud-Native**: Works seamlessly with cloud services\n- **Multi-Region**: Deploy across multiple regions\n- **High Availability**: 99.99% uptime SLA\n- **Disaster Recovery**: Automatic failover\n- **Backup**: Automated backups to cloud storage\n\n### 7. API Key Management\n\n#### API Key Features\n- **Key Generation**: Secure random key generation\n- **Key Rotation**: Automatic key rotation\n- **Key Revocation**: Immediate key revocation\n- **Key Scopes**: Limit key permissions\n- **Key Expiration**: Automatic expiration\n- **Key Usage Tracking**: Monitor key usage\n\n#### Key Types\n- **Service Keys**: For service-to-service communication\n- **User Keys**: For user authentication\n- **Admin Keys**: For administrative access\n- **Read-Only Keys**: Limited to read operations\n- **Temporary Keys**: Short-lived keys\n\n### 8. Certificate Management\n\n#### Certificate Features\n- **Certificate Generation**: Create SSL/TLS certificates\n- **Certificate Signing**: Internal CA for signing\n- **Certificate Renewal**: Automatic renewal\n- **Certificate Revocation**: Immediate revocation\n- **Certificate Monitoring**: Expiration alerts\n\n#### Certificate Types\n- **SSL/TLS Certificates**: Web server certificates\n- **Client Certificates**: Client authentication\n- **Code Signing**: Sign applications and scripts\n- **Email Certificates**: S/MIME certificates\n- **SSH Certificates**: SSH authentication\n\n#### Certificate Authorities\n- **Internal CA**: Self-signed certificates\n- **Let\'s Encrypt**: Free automated certificates\n- **DigiCert**: Commercial certificates\n- **Custom CA**: Bring your own CA\n\n---\n\n## üîå API Reference\n\n### Secret Management\n\n#### Create Secret\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/secrets\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "path": "database/production/postgres",\n  "data": {\n    "username": "db_user",\n    "password": "secure_password_123",\n    "host": "postgres.example.com",\n    "port": 5432\n  },\n  "metadata": {\n    "description": "Production database credentials",\n    "tags": ["production", "database"],\n    "rotation_enabled": true,\n    "rotation_period": "30d"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Read Secret\n```http\nGET /api/v1/secrets/database/production/postgres\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "path": "database/production/postgres",\n  "data": {\n    "username": "db_user",\n    "password": "secure_password_123",\n    "host": "postgres.example.com",\n    "port": 5432\n  },\n  "metadata": {\n    "version": 1,\n    "created_at": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z",\n    "updated_at": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Update Secret\n```http\nPUT /api/v1/secrets/database/production/postgres\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "data": {\n    "password": "new_secure_password_456"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Delete Secret\n```http\nDELETE /api/v1/secrets/database/production/postgres\n```\n\n#### List Secrets\n```http\nGET /api/v1/secrets?path=database/production\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "secrets": [\n    "database/production/postgres",\n    "database/production/mysql",\n    "database/production/redis"\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n### Dynamic Secrets\n\n#### Generate Database Credentials\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/dynamic/database/postgres\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "ttl": "1h",\n  "role": "readonly"\n}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "lease_id": "lease_abc123",\n  "username": "v-readonly-abc123",\n  "password": "temp_password_xyz789",\n  "expires_at": "2024-01-15T11:00:00Z"\n}\n```\n\n#### Renew Lease\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/dynamic/renew\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "lease_id": "lease_abc123",\n  "increment": "30m"\n}\n```\n\n#### Revoke Lease\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/dynamic/revoke\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "lease_id": "lease_abc123"\n}\n```\n\n### Secret Rotation\n\n#### Rotate Secret\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/secrets/database/production/postgres/rotate\n```\n\n#### Get Rotation Status\n```http\nGET /api/v1/secrets/database/production/postgres/rotation\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "enabled": true,\n  "period": "30d",\n  "last_rotation": "2024-01-01T00:00:00Z",\n  "next_rotation": "2024-01-31T00:00:00Z"\n}\n```\n\n### Access Policies\n\n#### Create Policy\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/policies\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "name": "database-readonly",\n  "rules": [\n    {\n      "path": "database/*",\n      "capabilities": ["read", "list"]\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n#### Assign Policy to User\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/users/{user_id}/policies\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "policies": ["database-readonly"]\n}\n```\n\n### Audit Logs\n\n#### Get Audit Logs\n```http\nGET /api/v1/audit/logs?start_date=2024-01-01&end_date=2024-01-31\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "logs": [\n    {\n      "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z",\n      "user": "user_123",\n      "action": "read",\n      "path": "database/production/postgres",\n      "ip_address": "192.168.1.100",\n      "success": true\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## üîß Configuration\n\n### Environment Variables\n\n```bash\n# Database Configuration\nVAULT_DB_HOST=localhost\nVAULT_DB_PORT=5432\nVAULT_DB_NAME=vault\nVAULT_DB_USER=vault_user\nVAULT_DB_PASSWORD=secure_password\n\n# Encryption Configuration\nVAULT_MASTER_KEY=base64_encoded_master_key\nVAULT_ENCRYPTION_ALGORITHM=AES-256-GCM\n\n# Storage Backend\nVAULT_STORAGE_BACKEND=postgresql\nVAULT_STORAGE_PATH=/vault/data\n\n# Enterprise Hub Integration\nVAULT_HUB_URL=http://enterprise-hub:8000\nVAULT_HUB_API_KEY=hub_api_key\nVAULT_HUB_ENABLED=true\n\n# Ninja Integration\nVAULT_NINJA_URL=http://ninja:8000\nVAULT_NINJA_API_KEY=ninja_api_key\nVAULT_NINJA_ENABLED=true\n\n# PassPort Integration\nVAULT_PASSPORT_URL=http://passport:8000\nVAULT_PASSPORT_API_KEY=passport_api_key\n\n# Audit Logging\nVAULT_AUDIT_ENABLED=true\nVAULT_AUDIT_LOG_PATH=/var/log/vault/audit.log\nVAULT_AUDIT_RETENTION_DAYS=90\n\n# High Availability\nVAULT_HA_ENABLED=true\nVAULT_HA_CLUSTER_ADDR=https://vault-1:8201\n\n# TLS Configuration\nVAULT_TLS_CERT_FILE=/certs/vault.crt\nVAULT_TLS_KEY_FILE=/certs/vault.key\nVAULT_TLS_CA_FILE=/certs/ca.crt\n\n# Logging\nVAULT_LOG_LEVEL=INFO\nVAULT_LOG_FORMAT=json\n```\n\n---\n\n## üöÄ Quick Start\n\n### Installation\n\n#### Using Docker\n```bash\n# Pull the image\ndocker pull itechsmart/vault:latest\n\n# Run the container\ndocker run -d \\\n  --name vault \\\n  -p 8200:8200 \\\n  -e VAULT_DB_HOST=postgres \\\n  -e VAULT_DB_PASSWORD=secure_password \\\n  -e VAULT_MASTER_KEY=$(openssl rand -base64 32) \\\n  itechsmart/vault:latest\n```\n\n#### Initialize Vault\n```bash\n# Initialize vault (first time only)\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:8200/api/v1/init\n\n# Unseal vault\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:8200/api/v1/unseal \\\n  -d \'{"key": "unseal_key_1"}\'\n```\n\n### Storing Your First Secret\n\n```python\nimport requests\n\n# Store a secret\nsecret = {\n    "path": "myapp/database",\n    "data": {\n        "username": "app_user",\n        "password": "secure_password"\n    }\n}\n\nresponse = requests.post(\n    "http://localhost:8200/api/v1/secrets",\n    json=secret,\n    headers={"Authorization": "Bearer YOUR_TOKEN"}\n)\n\n# Read the secret\nresponse = requests.get(\n    "http://localhost:8200/api/v1/secrets/myapp/database",\n    headers={"Authorization": "Bearer YOUR_TOKEN"}\n)\n\nsecret_data = response.json()["data"]\nprint(f"Password: {secret_data[\'password\']}")\n```\n\n---\n\n## üîó Integration Points\n\n### Enterprise Hub Integration\n- Centralized secret management\n- Cross-product secret sharing\n- Unified audit logging\n- Secret usage analytics\n\n### PassPort Integration\n- User authentication\n- Service authentication\n- Role-based access control\n- Multi-factor authentication\n\n### Ninja Integration\n- Security monitoring\n- Auto-rotation of compromised secrets\n- Performance optimization\n- Backup and recovery\n\n### All Product Integrations\n- **All iTechSmart Products**: Secure secret storage\n- **DataFlow**: Database credentials\n- **Connect**: API keys\n- **Shield**: Security keys\n- **Cloud**: Cloud credentials\n\n---\n\n## üìä 99.99%\n\n---\n\n## üîí Security\n\n### Security Features\n- AES-256 encryption\n- TLS 1.3 for all communications\n- Master key encryption\n- Key rotation\n- Audit logging\n- Access policies\n- IP whitelisting\n- Rate limiting\n\n### Compliance\n- SOC 2 Type II\n- HIPAA\n- PCI DSS\n- GDPR\n- ISO 27001\n\n---\n\n## üêõ Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n#### Vault Sealed\n```bash\n# Check seal status\ncurl http://localhost:8200/api/v1/seal-status\n\n# Unseal vault\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:8200/api/v1/unseal \\\n  -d \'{"key": "unseal_key"}\'\n```\n\n#### Permission Denied\n```bash\n# Check user policies\ncurl http://localhost:8200/api/v1/users/me/policies \\\n  -H "Authorization: Bearer YOUR_TOKEN"\n\n# Verify policy allows access\ncurl http://localhost:8200/api/v1/policies/policy_name\n```\n\n---\n\n## üìö Additional Resources\n\n- **API Documentation**: http://localhost:8200/docs\n- **User Guide**: shortening\n\n#### Push Notifications\n- **Mobile Push**: iOS (APNs) and Android (FCM)\n- **Web Push**: Browser notifications\n- **Rich Notifications**: Images, actions, sounds\n- **Silent Push**: Here are some products you might like.\n{% endif %}\n\n{% for product in recommended_products %}\n  - {{product.name}}: ${{product.price}}\n{% endfor %}\n```\n\n### 4. Rate Limiting\n\n#### Rate Limit Features\n- **Per User**: Limit notifications per user\n- **Per Channel**: Limit per channel\n- **Per Campaign**: Limit per campaign\n- **Global**: Overall rate limits\n- **Time Windows**: Hourly, daily, weekly\n- **Priority**: Prioritize important messages\n- **Quiet Hours**: Respect user preferences\n\n#### Rate Limit Strategies\n- **Fixed Window**: Fixed time periods\n- **Sliding Window**: Rolling time windows\n- **Token Bucket**: Burst handling\n- **Leaky Bucket**: Smooth rate limiting\n\n### 8. application/json\n\n{\n  "to": ["user@example.com"],\n  "template_id": "welcome_email",\n  "subject": "Welcome to {{company_name}}!",\n  "data": {\n    "user_name": "John Doe",\n    "company_name": "Acme Corp"\n  },\n  "attachments": [\n    {\n      "filename": "welcome.pdf",\n      "content": "base64_encoded_content"\n    }\n  ],\n  "tracking": {\n    "opens": true,\n    "clicks": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Send SMS\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/notifications/sms\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "to": ["+1234567890"],\n  "message": "Your verification code is {{code}}",\n  "data": {\n    "code": "123456"\n  },\n  "sender_id": "ACME"\n}\n```\n\n#### Send Push Notification\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/notifications/push\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "to": ["device_token_1", "device_token_2"],\n  "title": "New Message",\n  "body": "You have a new message from {{sender}}",\n  "data": {\n    "sender": "John Doe",\n    "message_id": "msg_123"\n  },\n  "badge": 1,\n  "sound": "default",\n  "deep_link": "app://messages/msg_123"\n}\n```\n\n#### Send Slack Message\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/notifications/slack\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "channel": "#general",\n  "text": "Deployment completed successfully!",\n  "blocks": [\n    {\n      "type": "section",\n      "text": {\n        "type": "mrkdwn",\n        "text": "*Deployment Status*\\nEnvironment: Production\\nStatus: ‚úÖ Success"\n      }\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n#### Send Teams Message\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/notifications/teams\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "channel": "General",\n  "title": "Build Notification",\n  "text": "Build #123 completed",\n  "theme_color": "00FF00",\n  "sections": [\n    {\n      "activityTitle": "Build Completed",\n      "activitySubtitle": "Production deployment",\n      "facts": [\n        {"name": "Status", "value": "Success"},\n        {"name": "Duration", "value": "5m 23s"}\n      ]\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n#### Send WhatsApp Message\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/notifications/whatsapp\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "to": "+1234567890",\n  "template": "order_confirmation",\n  "language": "en",\n  "parameters": [\n    {"type": "text", "text": "John Doe"},\n    {"type": "text", "text": "ORDER-123"}\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n### Template Management\n\n#### Create Template\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/templates\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "name": "welcome_email",\n  "channel": "email",\n  "subject": "Welcome to {{company_name}}!",\n  "body": "<h1>Welcome {{user_name}}!</h1><p>Thanks for joining us.</p>",\n  "variables": ["user_name", "company_name"]\n}\n```\n\n#### Get Template\n```http\nGET /api/v1/templates/{template_id}\n```\n\n### Delivery Status\n\n#### Get Notification Status\n```http\nGET /api/v1/notifications/{notification_id}/status\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "id": "notif_123",\n  "status": "delivered",\n  "channel": "email",\n  "sent_at": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z",\n  "delivered_at": /api/v1/analytics/campaigns/{campaign_id}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "campaign_id": "camp_123",\n  "sent": 10000,\n  "delivered": 9850,\n  "opened": 4500,\n  "clicked": 1200,\n  "converted": 300,\n  "open_rate": 0.457,\n  "click_rate": 0.122,\n  "conversion_rate": 0.030\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## üîß Configuration\n\n### Environment Variables\n\n```bash\n# Database        "company_name": "Acme Corp"\n    }\n}\n\nresponse = requests.post(\n    "http://localhost:8080/api/v1/notifications/email",\n    json=notification,\n    headers={"Authorization": "Bearer optimization\n- Backup and recovery\n\n**ProofLink Integration**:\n- Extends document verification\n- Blockchain-based proof of existence\n- Timestamped document hashes\n- Immutable document history\n\n**Standalone Mode**:\n- Can operate without Hub connection\n- Local blockchain node\n- File-based configuration\n- Offline audit trails\n\n---\n\n## üöÄ Core Features\n\n### 1. Blockchain-Based Audit Trails\n\n#### Audit Trail Features\n- **Immutable Records**: Cannot be modified or deleted\n- **Tamper Detection**: Cryptographic verification\n- **Complete History**: Full audit trail from creation\n- **Time-Ordered**: Chronological record keeping\n- **Distributed**: Replicated across multiple nodes\n- **Verifiable**: Anyone can verify authenticity\n- **Searchable**: Query audit trails efficiently\n- **Exportable**: Export for compliance\n\n#### Record Types\n- **Transaction Records**: Financial transactions\n- **Access Records**: Who accessed what and when\n- **Change Records**: Data modifications\n- **System Events**: System operations\n- **User Actions**: User activities\n- **API Calls**: API request/response logs\n- **Configuration Changes**: System configuration\n- **Security Events**: Security-related events\n\n#### Audit Trail Operations\n```python\n# Create audit record\n{\n  "event_type": "user_login",\n  "user_id": "user_123",\n  "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z",\n  "ip_address": "192.168.1.100",\n  "metadata": {\n    "user_agent": "Mozilla/5.0...",\n    "location": "New York, US"\n  }\n}\n\n# Verify audit record\n{\n  "record_id": "rec_abc123",\n  "hash": "sha256_hash",\n  "previous_hash": "sha256_previous_hash",\n  "block_number": 12345,\n  "verified": true\n}\n```\n\n### 2. Smart Contracts\n\n#### Smart Contract Features\n- **Automated Execution**: Execute business logic automatically\n- **Conditional Logic**: If-then-else conditions\n- **Multi-Party Agreements**: Multiple signatories\n- **Escrow**: Hold funds until conditions met\n- **Time-Based**: Execute at specific times\n- **Event-Driven**: Trigger on events\n- **Upgradeable**: Update contract logic\n- **Gas Optimization**: Efficient execution\n\n#### Contract Types\n- **Payment Contracts**: Automated payments\n- **Escrow Contracts**: Hold funds in escrow\n- **Supply Chain**: Track goods movement\n- **Identity Verification**: Verify identities\n- **Access Control**: Manage permissions\n- **Voting**: Decentralized voting\n- **Licensing**: Software licensing\n- **Insurance**: Automated claims\n\n#### Smart Contract Example\n```solidity\n// Simple escrow contract\ncontract Escrow {\n    address public buyer;\n    address public seller;\n    uint256 public amount;\n    bool public released;\n    \n    function deposit() public payable {\n        require(msg.sender == buyer);\n        amount = msg.value;\n    }\n    \n    function release() public {\n        require(msg.sender == buyer);\n        require(!released);\n        seller.transfer(amount);\n        released = true;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3. Cryptographic Verification\n\n#### Verification Features\n- **Digital Signatures**: Sign documents and transactions\n- **Hash Functions**: SHA-256, SHA-3, Blake2\n- **Public Key Infrastructure**: PKI support\n- **Certificate Authority**: Internal CA\n- **Signature Verification**: Verify signatures\n- **Multi-Signature**: Require multiple signatures\n- **Threshold Signatures**: M-of-N signatures\n- **Zero-Knowledge Proofs**: Prove without revealing\n\n#### Signature Types\n- **Document Signatures**: Sign PDF, Word, etc.\n- **Transaction Signatures**: Sign blockchain transactions\n- **API Signatures**: Sign API requests\n- **Email Signatures**: S/MIME signatures\n- **Code Signatures**: Sign software\n- **Timestamp Signatures**: Trusted timestamps\n\n### 4. Multi-Chain Support\n\n#### Supported Blockchains\n- **Public Chains**:\n  - Ethereum (ETH)\n  - Bitcoin (BTC)\n  - Polygon (MATIC)\n  - Binance Smart Chain (BSC)\n  - Avalanche (AVAX)\n  \n- **Private Chains**:\n  - Hyperledger Fabric\n  - Hyperledger Besu\n  - Quorum\n  - Corda\n  - Custom private chains\n\n#### Chain Features\n- **Multi-Chain Transactions**: Atomic swaps\n- **Cross-Chain Verification**: Verify across chains\n- **Chain Selection**: Choose optimal chain\n- **Gas Optimization**: Minimize transaction costs\n- **Chain Monitoring**: Monitor chain health\n\n### 5. Compliance Reporting\n\n#### Compliance Standards\n- **SOC 2**: SOC 2 Type II compliance\n- **HIPAA**: Healthcare compliance\n- **PCI DSS**: Payment card compliance\n- **GDPR**: Data privacy compliance\n- **ISO 27001**: Information security\n- **SOX**: Sarbanes-Oxley compliance\n- **FINRA**: Financial compliance\n- **21 CFR Part 11**: FDA compliance\n\n#### Report Types\n- **Audit Reports**: Complete audit trails\n- **Access Reports**: Who accessed what\n- **Change Reports**: What changed and when\n- **Security Reports**: Security events\n- **Compliance Reports**: Regulatory compliance\n- **Custom Reports**: Build custom reports\n\n#### Report Features\n- **Automated Generation**: Schedule reports\n- **Real-Time Reports**: Live compliance status\n- **Historical Reports**: Trend analysis\n- **Export Formats**: PDF, Excel, CSV, JSON\n- **Digital Signatures**: Sign reports\n- **Timestamping**: Timestamp reports\n\n### 6. Digital Signatures\n\n#### Signature Features\n- **Legally Binding**: Compliant with eIDAS, ESIGN\n- **Multi-Party Signing**: Multiple signatories\n- **Sequential Signing**: Sign in order\n- **Parallel Signing**: Sign simultaneously\n- **Signature Verification**: Verify authenticity\n- **Signature Revocation**: Revoke signatures\n- **Signature Audit Trail**: Track signing process\n- **Biometric Signatures**: Fingerprint, face ID\n\n#### Signature Workflows\n- **Simple Signing**: Single signer\n- **Multi-Party Signing**: Multiple signers\n- **Approval Workflows**: Hierarchical approval\n- **Witness Signing**: Witness signatures\n- **Notary Signing**: Notarized signatures\n\n### 7. Timestamping\n\n#### Timestamp Features\n- **Trusted Timestamps**: RFC 3161 compliant\n- **Blockchain Timestamps**: Immutable timestamps\n- **Batch Timestamping**: Timestamp multiple items\n- **Timestamp Verification**: Verify timestamps\n- **Timestamp Renewal**: Extend timestamp validity\n- **Long-Term Validation**: LTV support\n\n#### Timestamp Uses\n- **Document Timestamping**: Prove document existence\n- **Transaction Timestamping**: Timestamp transactions\n- **Log Timestamping**: Timestamp log entries\n- **Email Timestamping**: Timestamp emails\n- **Code Timestamping**: Timestamp software releases\n\n### 8. Data Provenance\n\n#### Provenance Features\n- **Origin Tracking**: Track data origin\n- **Transformation History**: Track data changes\n- **Lineage Visualization**: Visual data flow\n- **Impact Analysis**: Downstream impacts\n- **Dependency Mapping**: Data dependencies\n- **Quality Tracking**: Data quality metrics\n\n---\n\n## üîå API Reference\n\n### Audit Trail Management\n\n#### Create Audit Record\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/audit/records\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "event_type": "data_access",\n  "user_id": "user_123",\n  "resource_type": "customer_data",\n  "resource_id": "cust_456",\n  "action": "read",\n  "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z",\n  "metadata": {\n    "ip_address": "192.168.1.100",\n    "user_agent": "Mozilla/5.0..."\n  }\n}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "record_id": "rec_abc123",\n  "block_number": 12345,\n  "transaction_hash": "0x123abc...",\n  "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:00:01Z",\n  "verified": true\n}\n```\n\n#### Get Audit Record\n```http\nGET /api/v1/audit/records/{record_id}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "record_id": "rec_abc123",\n  "event_type": "data_access",\n  "user_id": "user_123",\n  "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z",\n  "block_number": 12345,\n  "transaction_hash": "0x123abc...",\n  "previous_hash": "0x456def...",\n  "verified": true\n}\n```\n\n#### Query Audit Trail\n```http\nGET /api/v1/audit/records?user_id=user_123&start_date=2024-01-01&end_date=2024-01-31\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "records": [\n    {\n      "record_id": "rec_abc123",\n      "event_type": "data_access",\n      "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z"\n    }\n  ],\n  "total": 150,\n  "page": 1,\n  "per_page": 50\n}\n```\n\n#### Verify Audit Record\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/audit/records/{record_id}/verify\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "record_id": "rec_abc123",\n  "verified": true,\n  "block_number": 12345,\n  "transaction_hash": "0x123abc...",\n  "verification_timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:05:00Z"\n}\n```\n\n### Smart Contracts\n\n#### Deploy Smart Contract\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/contracts/deploy\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "name": "Escrow Contract",\n  "code": "contract Escrow { ... }",\n  "parameters": {\n    "buyer": "0x123...",\n    "seller": "0x456...",\n    "amount": 1000\n  }\n}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "contract_id": "contract_abc123",\n  "address": "0x789...",\n  "transaction_hash": "0xabc...",\n  "deployed_at": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z"\n}\n```\n\n#### Execute Contract Function\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/contracts/{contract_id}/execute\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "function": "release",\n  "parameters": {},\n  "gas_limit": 100000\n}\n```\n\n### Digital Signatures\n\n#### Sign Document\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/signatures/sign\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "document_id": "doc_123",\n  "signer_id": "user_456",\n  "signature_type": "digital",\n  "certificate_id": "cert_789"\n}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "signature_id": "sig_abc123",\n  "document_id": "doc_123",\n  "signer_id": "user_456",\n  "signed_at": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z",\n  "signature_hash": "sha256_hash",\n  "verified": true\n}\n```\n\n#### Verify Signature\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/signatures/{signature_id}/verify\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "signature_id": "sig_abc123",\n  "valid": true,\n  "signer": "user_456",\n  "signed_at": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z",\n  "certificate_valid": true\n}\n```\n\n### Timestamping\n\n#### Create Timestamp\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/timestamps\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "data_hash": "sha256_hash_of_data",\n  "description": "Document timestamp"\n}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "timestamp_id": "ts_abc123",\n  "data_hash": "sha256_hash_of_data",\n  "timestamp": /api/v1/timestamps/{timestamp_id}/verify\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "timestamp_id": "ts_abc123",\n  "valid": true,\n  "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z",\n  "verified_at": "2024-01-15T10:05:00Z"\n}\n```\n\n### Compliance Reports\n\n#### Generate Compliance Report\n```http\nPOST /api/v1/compliance/reports\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "report_type": "soc2",\n itechsmart/ledger:latest\n```\n\n### Creating Your First Audit Record\n\n```python\nimport requests\n\n# Create an audit record\naudit_record = {\n    "event_type": "user_login",\n    "user_id": "user_123",\n    "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z",\n    "metadata": {\n        "ip_address": "192.168.1.100"\n    }\n}\n\nresponse = requests.post(\n    "http://localhost:8080/api/v1/audit/records",\n    json=audit_record,\n    headers={"Authorization": "Bearer YOUR_API_KEY"}\n)\n\nrecord_id = response.json()["record_id"]\nprint(f"Audit record created: {record_id}")\n\n# Verify the record\nverify_response = requests.post(\n    f"http://localhost:8080/api/v1/audit/records/{record_id}/verify",\n    headers={"Authorization": "Bearer YOUR_API_KEY"}\n)\n\nprint(f"Verified: {verify_response.json()[\'verified\']}")\n```\n\n---\n\n## üîó Integration Points\n\n### Enterprise Hub Integration\n- Centralized audit trail management\n-    "total_revenue": 1200000,\n    "growth": 0.15,\n    "top_product": "Product A"\n  },\n  "actions": [\n    {\n      "type": "show_chart",\n      "data": {...}\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n#### Get
